use master;
go
if exists(select * from sys.databases where name='Csdl_Sach')
drop database Csdl_Sach;
go
create database Csdl_Sach;
go
use Csdl_Sach;
go

-- Tao bang NHAXUATBAN
create table NHAXUATBAN (
	MaNXB		int not null, 
	TenNXB		varchar(255) not null,
  	constraint PK_NHAXUATBAN primary key (MaNXB)
);

-- Tao bang TACGIA
create table TACGIA ( 
	MaTG		int not null,
  	HoTG		varchar(100) not null,
	Dem		varchar(100), 
  	TenTG		varchar(100),
  	constraint PK_TACGIA primary key (MaTG)
);

-- Tao bang SACH
create table SACH (
  	MaSA		int not null, 
	TenSA		varchar(255) not null, 
  	SoTrang		int, 
  	XepHang		decimal(4, 2), 
  	ISBN		varchar(13), 
  	NgayXuatBan	date, 
  	MaNXB		int, 
  	constraint PK_SACH primary key (MaSA),
  	constraint FK_SACH foreign key (MaNXB) references NHAXUATBAN(maNXB)
);

-- Tao bang VIETSACH
create table VIETSACH (
  	MaSA		int not null, 
  	MaTG		int not null, 
  	constraint PK_VIETSACH primary key (MaSA, MaTG), 
  	constraint FK_VIETSACH_SACH foreign key (MaSA) references SACH(MaSA) on delete cascade, 
  	constraint FK_VIETSACH_TACGIA foreign key (MaTG) references TACGIA(MaTG) on delete cascade
);

-- Tao bang THELOAI
create table THELOAI (
  	MaTL		int not null,
  	TenTL		varchar(255) not null, 
  	ThuocTL		int, 
	constraint PK_THELOAI primary key (MaTL),
  	constraint FK_THELOAI foreign key (ThuocTL) references THELOAI(MaTL)
);

-- Tao bang LOAISACH
create table LOAISACH (
  	MaSA		int not null, 
  	MaTL		int not null, 
  	constraint PK_LOAISACH	primary key (MaSA, MaTL), 
  	constraint FK_LOAISACH_SACH foreign key (MaSA) references SACH(MaSA) on delete cascade, 
  	constraint FK_LOAISACH_THELOAI foreign key (MaTL) references THELOAI(MaTL) on delete cascade
);
